name:A‍n‍o‍n‍y‍m‍o‍u‍s‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r

posted:Posted February 14, 2024
msg:Address: After getting off the highway, there is a sign on the roadside not far away. Turn into the small road and there are two parking lots. The big parking lot is a bit far from the hotel, and the small one can't park a few cars. All the cars are parked on the roadside near the hotel.

Service: I arrived at almost 2 o'clock in the afternoon, but the room was not ready for check-in. I waited for more than half an hour before the room was ready for check-in. The attitude of the front desk staff was okay, but not very professional. The overall hotel did not experience the service quality that matched the price.

Room: We booked Japanese tatami that can be soaked indoors. The overall decoration is relatively old. Many of them have cracked, bulged, and discolored. The faucets and showers are also leaking on the sides. The only thing I am satisfied with is that the mattress is not bad. The central air conditioner will turn on automatically at night when I sleep, and the noise is still quite loud.

Hot spring: The hot spring time is until 11pm. We went there at 8pm. We changed into swimsuits in the room. The floor of the bathing area in the men's locker room was very dirty. I don't know if it was mud or hair. Many drains were blocked by hair. The shower water flow was relatively small, and some were broken. It was very cold after washing. There was no heating. There was only a gas heater at the door of the locker room. When you enter the indoor bathing area, you can smell the water vapor mixed with the smell of paint. The color of the water in the pool is also dark, with mud at the bottom. There are also many impurities in the outdoor water. The overall experience is not good. I didn't feel like soaking and went back to the room directly without going to the entertainment area.

Breakfast: Simple buffet, two points I want to complain about, one is that the fried dough sticks are obviously leftover, and they are very hard to bite after heating, and the second is that there are no glasses in the hot drink area in the restaurant after 8 o'clock, so you can only use paper cups. The taste of other meals is average.

Overall evaluation: The hotel facilities are old, the dynamic line is strange, the decoration is rough, the service is amateur, and the experience is extremely poor. The price was over 1,300 RMB when I booked it before the Chinese New Year, but it had risen to over 1,600 RMB on the day. What I was most dissatisfied with was that after spending so much money, the overall experience was totally not worth the price. I chose the most expensive one in Bazhou at that time, thinking that spending more money would always have its own reasons, but I was totally ripped off.

msg:Overall, it was a pleasant surprise! My father had just recovered from a serious illness and could not travel far, so we decided to soak in hot springs nearby. However, we could not book anything in the ancient town of Mobei.
First of all, I would like to thank Ctrip customer service! We failed to book the ancient town of Mobei several times, but Ctrip customer service was very considerate. When the booking failed, they even gave us a cash voucher.
Then, according to the recommendation of Ctrip app, we went to Bazhou, which was only 100 km away. For the same price, it included hot springs and buffet.
(1) Convenient transportation. If you are going from Beijing, don’t drive too close or too smoothly. It is only 5 km away after getting off the highway. There are many parking spaces in the hotel, and the parking lot is full of Beijing cars.
(2) Hot springs. It is really good. I haven’t seen a real hot spring for a long time. It is very comfortable. It’s just that there are more people bathing in the afternoon, but if you stay in the hotel, you can bathe in the morning or evening to avoid peak hours, hahahaha. In addition, the outdoor hot springs are great!
(3) Hotel service. Well, the service staff are very enthusiastic and have a good attitude, but I guess they have never received so many people before and were overwhelmed. . .
(4) Self-service. The room includes meals, breakfast + lunch/dinner. We had dinner. It was not a big meal, but it was definitely good. My parents also enjoyed the meal. It was a comfortable meal for everyone, young and old. In addition, I have to say that the hotel is very generous. Drinks are not served in cups, but in bottles. Korla pears and Baba oranges are all whole.
(5) Surroundings. There is nothing around. It is 5 kilometers away from the entrance of Bazhou City Government. There is a night market with various food. There is also a Haiyue Shopping Mall nearby. It is a bit big and looks good. After breakfast the next day, we went to Shengfang Ancient Town. There was a temple fair. Although it was a bit low-end, the kids had a lot of fun. I didn’t expect that the ancient town has a long history. I remember it as early as the Spring and Autumn Period.
(6) Others. Bathing and spa are cost-effective. Although they are different from Shenyang Bathing Center, I am generally satisfied. P.S. The spa lady’s technique is really good and powerful.
(7) Disadvantages. The indoor hot spring area is not very large. The shower in the room has been repaired twice, but I still can’t pee completely. . . Later, we all went to the female hot spring bathroom to take a bath. In addition, there are not enough public areas, so if you don't stay overnight, the experience will be worse.

posted:Posted January 27, 2024
msg:First of all, the geographical location is 1 hour and 30 minutes drive from Beijing, which is quite convenient. We arrived on Friday night and went to soak in the outdoor hot springs first. They were still under repair, and an excavator was parked around the pool. It was simply... There are about 5-6 outdoor hot springs, and the water temperature is around 40 degrees, which is still very comfortable. Apart from the construction factors, it is still very suitable for watching the moon at night. There is a private hot spring pool indoors, which is about 1.5 meters long and 1.2 meters wide. It can be bigger. The water quality and environment are very good, but the sound of the central air conditioner is like driving an old tractor, rumbling and making people unable to sleep. When sleeping, you can only turn it off and spend a night on the switch. I thought I could sleep until 12 o'clock, but I didn't expect that the decoration would start before 8 o'clock in the morning. The sound of electric drills and hammers, squeaking, booming, and booming, I had to coordinate with the hotel customer service 3 times before it stopped. I couldn't sleep, so I went to have breakfast. The breakfast is free when you check in, and the variety is very rich. I really want to give a thumbs up here. But the table in a good restaurant is uneven, and the plates are mostly chipped, which is easy to hurt your hands. And it was very cold, there was no air conditioning, so friends who plan to go there in winter must wear down jackets when eating breakfast. After breakfast, I returned to the room and started to hear the sound of electric drills and hammers. I coordinated with the hotel again, but it was still not resolved. Their process is that the customer service gives feedback to the manager, the manager gives feedback to the construction unit, the construction unit gives feedback to the contractor, the contractor finds the workers again, and the workers still insist on drilling. I had no choice but to complain to Ctrip and change the room. Here are some suggestions.
1. The hotel facilities are good, and the environment is like a new start-up
2. The service needs a lot of room for improvement. We checked in at 10 o'clock on Friday night, and there are still many vacant rooms and rooms in areas outside the construction. Can we give priority allocation or upgrade directly? Improve the experience to a higher level.
3. The breakfast is great. Can the infrastructure be improved? Have you ever seen a broken plate in a star-level hotel?
4. Can the efficiency be improved in solving customer complaints? A total of 10 calls took 2 hours to solve the problem. Can it be solved in 1 call and 2 minutes?
5. The hot and cold water signs in the rooms that have been switched are also reversed. Similar details can be checked regularly in each room.

msg:每年冬季都會來一兩次。房間還是老樣子，設施很老。最不能接受的還是屋內沒法洗澡🚿，花灑很小，水流更小。這次去房間贈送了香薰和海鹽泡温泉用。對於一千左右的價位來説和屋內環境設施不太相匹配。不過老公感覺還可以。這回是我第一次趕上週末去，人很多。最不能理解的是餐廳八點半就關門了。最後開車去霸州市裡麪吃的。因為穿着浴袍，餐廳不讓進，説要穿衣服。當時都8點了，上樓換完衣服就關門了。個人覺得，週末人多，應該晚一些關門。再説説這回最讓我不滿意的就是搓澡和按摩，每次去搓澡是必須的，這回真的給我弄疼了，而且我説了好幾次輕一些，最後我的身上還是有地方破了。之前的人就不會出現這個問題。這回做了個足底按摩，因為以前來做過兩次。真的很好。這次就很失望，還是搓澡的人做足底。我和老公選的198的，按摩的人戴上一次性手套，抹上磨砂膏就是搓啊，極少按穴位。總共60分鐘，就是磨砂膏一個勁的摸，然後搓腳。後來簡單的按按頭，胳膊和腿。肩頸按了兩下，腹部沒有按，就完事了。真心不是花不起錢，而是不能這麼糊弄人。兩人給我們按摩的時候，還一直聊天説，以前的客人有錢，做什麼項目都要貴的，現在的客人消費不行了等等。我想説，如果你們真的專業，服務的好，該消費還是會有很多人消費的。本身去那裡就是放鬆享受去了。但是我們也不傻啊，就這樣還怎麼能讓人去消費。完事了，結賬催着挺緊，我這還沒起身呢，他們手機二維碼就給我放這讓我掃。知道疫情這幾年能抗下來不容易，但是也希望你們別讓老客人太失望了。

msg:國慶假期哪兒都人多，所以帶孩子來泡個温泉。早就關注過他家，但前兩年因為疫情一直沒有成行。
設施：設備相對比較陳舊，但是都能正常使用。説一下空調，自己房間無法控制空調模式及温度，衹能控制打開關閉和風量，而且我住的房間沒有窗户，所以感覺空氣流通不是很好。花灑不太好用，出水量有些小，別的還可以。
環境：私湯温泉確實不錯，酒店裡也有好多室外温泉，水很乾凈。泳池有室內和室外的，室內的沒有室外的水好。室外是個無邊小泳池，孩子特別喜歡。
衞生：整體來説衞生條件不錯，衞生間也沒有異味。吐槽一下衞生間的設計，衞生間很大，因為裡邊有私湯，但是兩個地漏都不好使，洗完澡地上總會積留一些水，半天才能下去。
服務：重點説一下服務，他家的服務還是真的不錯。每天下午有個免費下午茶自助，孩子也是很喜歡。有蛋糕，飲料，咖啡和水果，還有自費的冰激凌和烤腸，很受歡迎。第一天入住，發現地漏堵了而且空調出風口不停的往下掉冷凝水，和工作人員溝通後，馬上給換了房間。
整體來説住宿體驗不錯，下次還會來！

name:R‍u‍o‍q‍i‍u‍l‍i‍n
info:Chinese-Style Superior Room
info:Stayed in January 2023
info:Family
info:11 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted January 28, 2023
msg:先説優點：
1.離北京近，開車一小時就能到，途徑大興動物園，可以順路玩
2.温泉不錯，屋內私湯跑的很舒服，公共的浴場分室內外，也很好。室外可以一邊看飛機一邊泡湯
3.有日式和中式房間，這次各訂了一間。體感中式更寬敞，但日式可以滿地打滾
4.價格不貴，房間含早，自助晚餐96一位，味道還行
5.安排了很多活動，包括做燈花、做年饃等等
幾個問題：
1.設施有點舊，而且衞生間沒有做到分離，帶孩子的話，上廁所私隱不太好
2.服務態度好，但服務水平不夠。想約個SPA，結果一共就2個技師，而且手法比較一般。
3.小童設施少，包括小童浴袍、拖鞋數量有時也不夠
4.市內不能放炮

name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Japanese-Style Standard Room
info:Stayed in March 2023

rating:5
posted:Posted March 15, 2023
msg:全5星好評主要是針對服務人員的熱情服務的，確實態度都很和善。但設施上確實需要進步了。
我七，八年前就多次住過這家，那個時候新建的，硬件設施好，這次主要發現設施維護情況不太理想，比如，房間的温泉池，邊沿上有螞蟻窩，晚上睡覺房間內居然有臭蟲。舊一些關係不大，但出現這種情況就是這個層次酒店該有的了。圖就不貼了，會讓看到的觀眾感受很差，店家可以自行進房間核實，畢竟我沒打差評。
總之，疫情三年可能是設施投入不足的原因，但目前的設施跟不上酒店對自己的定位了。
餐飲方面，早餐水準基本達標。自己點餐的價格不低，但水平比之前感覺退步了，尚可。
最後是是否推薦。我還是推薦帶孩子的家庭來玩的，但房間自己注意點我説的情況，公共設施方面，游泳池還維護不錯，室外温泉也有設施維護不佳的問題，小童空間比較小，但可以一玩，水邊的沙灘到夏天應該有可玩性，夏天來玩更佳。

不足之處:
1.房間冬日不夠温暖，靠空調續命的；
2.水龍頭老舊了，花灑堵塞，而且洗手盆的水龍頭管子也太短了，不好接水。

msg:怎麼説呢，真是一言難盡，沒有服務，沒有環境，和三亞的酒店比簡直差到極致，價格和三亞平日價格一樣了，沒有能力接待這麼多客人，不提前規劃好，配套服務設施都跟不上。春節過去住，晚上過海鮮自助，結果什麼沒有，衹有蝦還不是新鮮的，每人給了一個券衹能領一個扇貝和一個鮑魚，真是醉了，這破玩意也不值錢，真是諾大的酒店一點格局沒有，户外温泉，就幾個小池子，每個池子衹能泡4個人，就擁擠了，小童配套也跟不上，有個小淘氣堡還沒我家卧室大且無人管理又臟又亂。屋內更別提了，老舊到不成，地板也特別臟，這的好評絕對是刷出來的。一點都不如固安的建國酒店，不出京還不如昌平的樂多港温泉酒店，這麼遠過來，失望至極，服務人員一問三不知，懷疑春節人太多臨時過來幫忙的，自助餐發扇貝鮑魚的大哥，一看就不專業，態度蠻橫，而且竟然沒人領取的時候在旁邊抽電子煙，一點服務的樣兒也沒有，管理混亂，排隊的時候好多人罵這，估計都特別後悔來，總之不會再去第二次，而且排隊時大家聊天都這麼想的，太坑，太差勁了

msg:🍃環境：温泉外部環境整體還是不錯的 綠化面積很大 

🧹衞生：衹評價客房內的衞生 乍一看 不錯 但是由於裝修時間過早 導致現在設施比較老舊 電視櫃底下的土 也沒有清理過 如果單純衹是為了泡湯 可以選擇  其他理由是真的不推薦 房間內設備設施老化 也沒有冰箱  
關於疫情期間的出行 酒店整體給人的第一感覺是 根本不需要戴口罩 服務人員也不戴口罩 防疫意識太差 
定酒店入住 就會推薦你買餐廳套餐 將近400塊錢 一定不要被忽悠了 要果斷拒絕 
總結：適合單純泡湯的人來 如果有房間和環境的要求 那最好不要定了 不推薦

info:Chinese-Style Superior Room
info:Stayed in January 2024
info:Other
info:3 Reviews
rating:1
posted:Posted January 20, 2024
msg:本來預訂兩天酒店，第一天到酒店直接取消第二天行程，酒店的環境比較差，門的門鎖鎖不上，衹能掛鏈條鎖，門框還有裂痕，隔音很差，晚上還有找不到房間來刷我房間門鎖的客人。
最重要的是酒店房間內沒有任何關於地板損失賠償的告知，且辦理入住時無任何提示告知排水系統不行，入住後因酒店排水系統問題，導致地板浸水，第二天離店時強制不讓客人走，要求索賠，費用高昂，同時酒店方拒絕攜程調解，攜程建議我走法律程序，本來想回房間再核實下相關情況，但服務人員堅決不讓回房，僅給出高昂價目表，最終因為實在耗不起時間且不想再糾纏，賠償了費用2000元，趕緊離開。
後續經查詢，該酒店門頭未掛營業執照拍照，企查查系統顯示該公司已經被限制高消費，法人為被執行人，同時有很多司法訴訟，合計六千萬元，已經12315進行了投訴，大家還是不要去了。
